Authorizer implementation starts loading its metadata.</li>\\n51:  *   <li>Broker starts SocketServer to accept connections and process requests.</li>\\n52:  *   <li>For each listener, SocketServer waits for authorization metadata to be available in the\\n53:  *       authorizer before accepting connections. The future returned by {@link #start(AuthorizerServerInfo)}\\n54:  *       for each listener must return only when authorizer is ready to authorize requests on the listener.</li>\\n55:  *   <li>Broker accepts connections. For each connection, broker performs authentication and then accepts Kafka requests.\\n56:  *       For each request, broker invokes {@link #authorize(AuthorizableRequestContext, List)} to authorize\\n57:  *       actions performed by the request.</li>\\n58:  * </ol>\\n59:  *\\n60:  * Authorizer implementation class may optionally implement @{@link org.apache.kafka.common.Reconfigurable}\\n61:  * to enable dynamic reconfiguration without restarting the broker.\\n62:  * <p>Authorizer implementation class may also optionally implement {@link org.apache.kafka.common.metrics.Monitorable}\\n63:  * to enable the authorizer to register metrics. The following tags are automatically added to all metrics registered:\\n64:  * <code>config</code> set to <code>authorizer.class.name</code>, <code>class</code> set to the Authorizer class name,\\n65:  * and <code>role</code> set to either <code>broker</code> or <code>controller</code>.\\n66:  * <p>\\n67:  * <b>Threading model:</b>\\n68:  * <ul>\\n69:  *   <li>All authorizer operations including authorization and ACL updates must be thread-safe.</li>\\n70:  *   <li>ACL update methods are asynchronous. Implementations with low update latency may return a\\n71:  *       completed future using {@link java.util.concurrent.CompletableFuture#completedFuture(Object)}.\\n72:  *       This ensures that the request will be handled synchronously by the caller without using a\\n73:  *       purgatory to wait for the result. If ACL updates require remote communication which may block,\\n74:  *       return a future that is completed asynchronously when the remote operation completes. This enables\\n75:  *       the caller to process other requests on the request threads without blocking.</li>\\n76:  *   <li>Any threads or thread pools used for processing remote operations asynchronously can be started during\\n77:  *       {@link #start(AuthorizerServerInfo)}. These threads must be shutdown during {@link Authorizer#close()}.</li>\\n78:  * </ul>\\n79:  * </p>\\n80:  */\\n81: public interface Authorizer extends Configurable, Closeable {\\n82: \\n83:     /**\\n84:      * Starts loading authorization metadata and returns futures that can be used to wait until\\n85:      * metadata for authorizing requests on each listener is available. Each listener will be\\n86:      * started only after its metadata is available and authorizer is ready to start authorizing\\n87:      * requests on that listener.\\n88:      *\\n89:      * @param serverInfo Metadata for the broker including broker id and listener endpoints\\n90:      * @return CompletionStage for each endpoint that completes when authorizer is ready to\\n91:      *         start authorizing requests on that listener.\\n92:      */\\n93:     Map<Endpoint, ? extends CompletionStage<Void>> start(AuthorizerServerInfo serverInfo);\\n94: \\n95:     /**\\n96:      * Authorizes the specified action. Additional metadata for the action is specified\\n97:      * in `requestContext`.\\n98:      * <p>\\n99:      * This is a synchronous API designed for use with locally cached ACLs. Since this method is invoked on the\\n100:      * request thread while processing each request, implementations of this method should avoid time-consuming\\n101:      * remote communication that may block request threads.\\n102:      *\\n103:      * @param requestContext Request context including request type, security protocol and listener name\\n104:      * @param actions Actions being authorized including resource and operation for each action\\n105:      * @return List of authorization results for each action in the same order as the provided actions\\n106:      */\\n107:     List<AuthorizationResult> authorize(AuthorizableRequestContext requestContext, List<Action> actions);\\n108: \\n109:     /**\\n110:      * Creates new ACL bindings.\\n111:      * <p>\\n112:      * This is an asynchronous API that enables the caller to avoid blocking during the update. Each result\\n121:      *         is returned as a CompletionStage that completes when the result is available.\\n122:      */\\n123:     List<? extends CompletionStage<AclCreateResult>> createAcls(AuthorizableRequestContext requestContext, List<AclBinding> aclBindings);\\n124: \\n125:     /**\\n126:      * Deletes all ACL bindings that match the provided filters.\\n127:      * <p>\\n128:      * This is an asynchronous API that enables the caller to avoid blocking during the update. Implementations of this\\n129:      * API can return completed futures using {@link java.util.concurrent.CompletableFuture#completedFuture(Object)}\\n130:      * to process the update synchronously on the request thread.\\n131:      * <p>\\n132:      * Refer to the authorizer implementation docs for details on concurrent update guarantees.\\n133:      *\\n134:      * @param requestContext Request context if the ACL is being deleted by a broker to handle\\n135:      *        a client request to delete ACLs.\\n136:      * @param aclBindingFilters Filters to match ACL bindings that are to be deleted\\n137:      *\\n138:      * @return Delete result for each filter in the same order as in the input list.\\n139:      *         Each result indicates which ACL bindings were actually deleted as well as any\\n140:      *         bindings that matched but could not be deleted. Each result is returned as a\\n141:      *         CompletionStage that completes when the result is available.\\n142:      */\\n143:     List<? extends CompletionStage<AclDeleteResult>> deleteAcls(AuthorizableRequestContext requestContext, List<AclBindingFilter> aclBindingFilters);\\n144: \\n145:     /**\\n146:      * Returns ACL bindings which match the provided filter.\\n147:      * <p>\\n148:      * This is a synchronous API designed for use with locally cached ACLs. Authorizers that don't implement this function\\n158:      * will simply return -1.\\n159:      */\\n160:     default int aclCount() {\\n161:         return -1;\\n162:     }\\n163: \\n164:     /**\\n165:      * Check if the caller is authorized to perform the given ACL operation on at least one\\n166:      * resource of the given type.\\n167:      *\\n168:      * Custom authorizer implementations should consider overriding this default implementation because:\\n169:      * 1. The default implementation iterates all AclBindings multiple times, without any caching\\n170:      *    by principal, host, operation, permission types, and resource types. More efficient\\n171:      *    implementations may be added in custom authorizers that directly access cached entries.\\n172:      * 2. The default implementation cannot integrate with any audit logging included in the\\n173:      *    authorizer implementation.\\n174:      * 3. Return {@link AuthorizationResult#DENIED} otherwise.\\n183:      */\\n184:     default AuthorizationResult authorizeByResourceType(AuthorizableRequestContext requestContext, AclOperation op, ResourceType resourceType) {\\n185:         SecurityUtils.authorizeByResourceTypeCheckArgs(op, resourceType);\\n186: \\n187:         // Check a hard-coded name to ensure that super users are                     put(PatternType.PREFIXED, new HashSet<>());\\n212:                 }};\\n213: \\n214:         boolean hasWildCardAllow = false;\\n215: \\n216:         KafkaPrincipal principal = allowPatterns.get(PatternType.PREFIXED).add(binding.pattern().name());\\n262:                     break;\\n263:                 default:\\n264:             }\\n265:         }\\n266: \\n267:         if allow.\\n272:         // For any prefix allowed, if there's no dominant prefix denied, return allow.\\n273:         for (Map.Entry<PatternType, Set<String>> entry : allowPatterns.entrySet()) {\\n274:             }\\n287:                 if (!hasDominatedDeny)\\n288:                     return AuthorizationResult.ALLOWED;\\n289:             }\\n290:         }\\n291: \\n292:         return
